For status updates\n    finished_signal = pyqtSignal(bool, str)  # success, message\n\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__()\n        self._stop_requested = False\n\n    def request_stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Request the worker to stop.\"\"\"\n        self._stop_requested = True\n\n    def _download_file(self, url: str, destination: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Download a file from URL to destination.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            logger.debug(f\"Downloading {url} to {destination}\")\n            request = urllib.request.Request(\n                url,\n                headers={'User-Agent': 'Install-Scripts-GUI/1.0'}\n            )\n            with urllib.request.urlopen(request, timeout=30) as response:\n                content = response.read()\n\n            # Ensure directory exists\n            os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(destination), exist_ok=True)\n\n            with open(destination, 'wb') as f:\n                f.write(content)\n\n            logger.debug(f\"Successfully downloaded {url}\")\n            return True\n\n        except urllib.error.URLError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"URL error downloading {url}: {e}\")\n            return False\n        except urllib.error.HTTPError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"HTTP error downloading {url}: {e.code} {e.reason}\")\n            return False\n        except IOError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"IO error saving {destination}: {e}\")\n            return False\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Unexpected error downloading {url}: {e}\")\n            return False\n\n    def _get_scripts_list(self) -> List[Dict[str, str]]:\n        \"\"\"Get list of scripts from GitHub API.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            request = urllib.request.Request(\n                GITHUB_API_SCRIPTS,\n                headers={\n                    'User-Agent': 'Install-Scripts-GUI/1.0',\n                    'Accept': 'application/vnd.github.v3+json'\n                }\n            )\n            with urllib.request.urlopen(request, timeout=30) as response:\n                data = json.loads(response.read().decode('utf-8'))\n\n            # Filter for .sh files\n            scripts = []\n            for item in data:\n                if item.get('type') == 'file' and item.get('name', '').endswith('.sh'):\n                    scripts.append({\n                        'name': item['name'],\n                        'download_url': item['download_url']\n                    })\n\n            logger.debug(f\"Found {len(scripts)} scripts on GitHub\")\n            return scripts\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error fetching scripts list: {e}\")\n            return []\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"Download data files and scripts from GitHub.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            local_data_dir = get_local_data_dir()\n            local_scripts_dir = get_local_scripts_dir()\n            downloaded_count = 0\n            error_count = 0\n\n            # Step 1: Download data files\n            for data_file in DATA_FILES:\n                if self._stop_requested:\n                    self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Update cancelled')\n                    return\n\n                self.progress_signal.emit(data_file)\n                url = f\"{GITHUB_RAW_BASE}/{data_file}\"\n                destination = os.path.join(local_data_dir, data_file)\n\n                if self._download_file(url, destination):\n                    downloaded_count += 1\n                else:\n                    error_count += 1\n\n            # Step 2: Get scripts list from GitHub API\n            if self._stop_requested:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Update cancelled')\n                return\n\n            self.progress_signal.emit('scripts list')\n            scripts = self._get_scripts_list()\n\n            if not scripts:\n                # If API fails, try to get scripts from data files\n                logger.warning(\"Could not get scripts list from API, using data files\")\n            else:\n                # Step 3: Download each script\n                for script in scripts:\n                    if self._stop_requested:\n                        self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Update cancelled')\n                        return\n\n                    script_name = script['name']\n                    self.progress_signal.emit(script_name)\n                    destination = os.path.join(local_scripts_dir, script_name)\n\n                    if self._download_file(script['download_url'], destination):\n                        downloaded_count += 1\n                    else:\n                        error_count += 1\n\n            # Report results\n            if error_count > 0:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(\n                    False,\n                    f'Completed with {error_count} errors. Downloaded {downloaded_count} files.'\n                )\n            else:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(\n                    True,\n                    f'Successfully downloaded {downloaded_count} files.'\n                )\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Update error: {e}\")\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, str(e))\n\n\nclass MainWindow(QMainWindow):\n    \"\"\"Main application window.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, lang: str = DEFAULT_LANG):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.lang = lang\n        self.tr = TRANSLATIONS.get(lang, TRANSLATIONS[DEFAULT_LANG])\n        self.scripts = load_scripts(lang)\n        self.worker = None\n        self.update_worker = None\n        self._scripts_load_error = len(self.scripts) == 0\n\n        logger.debug(f\"MainWindow initialized with {len(self.scripts)} scripts\")\n\n        self.init_ui()\n\n    def init_ui(self):\n        \"\"\"Initialize the user interface.\"\"\"\n        self.setWindowTitle(self.tr['window_title'])\n        self.setMinimumSize(800, 600)\n\n        # Check each octet is 0-255\n        octets = ip.split('.')\n        return all(0 <= int(octet) <= 255 for octet in octets)\n\n    def on_script_selection_changed(self, index: int):\n        \"\"\"Handle script selection change in dropdown.\"\"\"\n        if index < 0 or index >= len(self.scripts):\n            self.description_label.setPlainText(\"\")\n            return\n\n        script = self.software_combo.itemData(index)\n        if script:\n            description = script.get('description', '')\n            info = script.get('info', '')\n            # Format: description on first line, info on second line (if present)\n            if info:\n                self.description_label.setPlainText(f\"{description}\\n\\n{info}\")\n            else:\n                self.description_label.setPlainText(description)\n\n    def on_install_clicked(self):\n        \"\"\"Handle install button click.\"\"\"\n        # Get selected script from combo box\n        current_index = self.software_combo.currentIndex()\n        if current_index < 0:\n            QMessageBox.warning(self, \"Error\", self.tr['error_no_script'])\n            return\n\n        script = self.software_combo.itemData(current_index)\n        if not script:\n            QMessageBox.warning(self, \"Error\", self.tr['error_no_script'])\n            return\n\n        script_name = script.get('script_name', '')\n        additional = self.additional_input.text().strip()\n\n        # operations.\"\"\"\n\n    output_received = pyqtSignal(str)\n    status_changed = pyqtSignal(str)\n    finished_signal = pyqtSignal(bool, str)\n\n    def __init__(self, server_ip: str, password: str, script_name: str,\n                 additional: str = '', port: int = SSH_DEFAULT_PORT):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.server_ip = server_ip\n        self.password = password\n        self.script_name = script_name\n        self.additional = additional\n        self.port = port\n        self._stop_requested = False\n        self._ssh_client = None\n\n    def request_stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Request the worker to stop.\"\"\"\n        self._stop_requested = True\n        if self._ssh_client:\n            try:\n                self._ssh_client.close()\n            except Exception:\n                pass\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"Execute the installation script via SSH.\"\"\"\n        if not SSH_AVAILABLE:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'SSH library (paramiko) is not installed')\n            return\n\n        try:\n            # Create SSH client\n            self._ssh_client = paramiko.SSHClient()\n            self._ssh_client.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())\n\n            self.status_changed.emit(f\"Connecting to {self.server_ip}:{self.port}...\")\n            self.output_received.emit(f\"Connecting to {self.server_ip}:{self.port} via SSH...\\n\")\n\n            # Connect to the server\n            self._ssh_client.connect(\n                hostname=self.server_ip,\n                port=self.port,\n                username='root',\n                password=self.password,\n                timeout=SSH_DEFAULT_TIMEOUT,\n                look_for_keys=False,\n                allow_agent=False\n            )\n\n            if self._stop_requested:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Stopped by user')\n                return\n\n            # Build the command\n            script_url = f\"{SCRIPTS_BASE_URL}/{self.script_name}.sh\"\n\n            if self.additional:\n                escaped_additional = self.additional.replace(\"'\", \"'\\\"'\\\"'\")\n                command = f\"curl -fsSL -o- {script_url} | bash -s -- '{escaped_additional}'\"\n            else:\n                command = f\"curl -fsSL -o- {script_url} | bash\"\n\n            self.output_received.emit(f\"Executing script: {self.script_name}\\n\")\n            self.output_received.emit(\"-\" * 50 + \"\\n\")\n\n            # Execute the command\n            stdin, stdout, stderr = self._ssh_client.exec_command(command, get_pty=True)\n\n            # Stream output\n            while True:\n                if self._stop_requested:\n                    self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Stopped by user')\n                    return\n\n                line = stdout.readline()\n                if not line:\n                    break\n\n                decoded_line = line if isinstance(line, str) else line.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')\n                clean_line = strip_ansi_codes(decoded_line)\n                self.output_received.emit(clean_line)\n\n            # Read any remaining stderr\n            error_output = stderr.read().decode('utf-8', errors='replace')\n            if error_output:\n                clean_error = strip_ansi_codes(error_output)\n                self.output_received.emit(f\"\\n{clean_error}\")\n\n            # Get exit status\n            exit_status = stdout.channel.recv_exit_status()\n\n            if exit_status != 0:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(False, f'Script exited with status {exit_status}')\n            else:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(True, 'Installation completed successfully')\n\n        except paramiko.AuthenticationException:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'SSH authentication failed. Please check the password.')\n        except paramiko.SSHException as e:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, f'SSH connection error: {str(e)}')\n        except TimeoutError:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, f'Connection to {self.server_ip} timed out')\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, f'Unexpected error: {str(e)}')\n        finally:\n            if self._ssh_client:\n                try:\n                    self._ssh_client.close()\n                except Exception:\n                    pass\n\n\nclass UpdateWorker(QThread):\n    \"\"\"Worker thread for downloading updates from GitHub.\"\"\"\n\n    progress_signal = pyqtSignal(str)  # For status updates\n    finished_signal = pyqtSignal(bool, str)  # success, message\n\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__()\n        self._stop_requested = False\n\n    def request_stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Request the worker to stop.\"\"\"\n        self._stop_requested = True\n\n    def _download_file(self, url: str, destination: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Download a file from URL to destination.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            logger.debug(f\"Downloading {url} to {destination}\")\n            request = urllib.request.Request(\n                url,\n                headers={'User-Agent': 'Install-Scripts-GUI/1.0'}\n            )\n            with urllib.request.urlopen(request, timeout=30) as response:\n                content = response.read()\n\n            # Ensure directory exists\n            os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(destination), exist_ok=True)\n\n            with open(destination, 'wb') as f:\n                f.write(content)\n\n            logger.debug(f\"Successfully downloaded {url}\")\n            return True\n\n        except urllib.error.URLError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"URL error downloading {url}: {e}\")\n            return False\n        except urllib.error.HTTPError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"HTTP error downloading {url}: {e.code} {e.reason}\")\n            return False\n        except IOError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"IO error saving {destination}: {e}\")\n            return False\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Unexpected error downloading {url}: {e}\")\n            return False\n\n    def _get_scripts_list(self) -> List[Dict[str, str]]:\n        \"\"\"Get list of scripts from GitHub API.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            request = urllib.request.Request(\n                GITHUB_API_SCRIPTS,\n                headers={\n                    'User-Agent': 'Install-Scripts-GUI/1.0',\n                    'Accept': 'application/vnd.github.v3+json'\n                }\n            )\n            with urllib.request.urlopen(request, timeout=30) as response:\n                data = json.loads(response.read().decode('utf-8'))\n\n            # Filter for .sh files\n            scripts = []\n            for item in data:\n                if item.get('type') == 'file' and item.get('name', '').endswith('.sh'):\n                    scripts.append({\n                        'name': item['name'],\n                        'download_url': item['download_url']\n                    })\n\n            logger.debug(f\"Found {len(scripts)} scripts on GitHub\")\n            return scripts\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error fetching scripts list: {e}\")\n            return []\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"Download data files and scripts from GitHub.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            local_data_dir = get_local_data_dir()\n            local_scripts_dir = get_local_scripts_dir()\n            downloaded_count = 0\n            error_count = 0\n\n            # Step 1: Download data files\n            for data_file in DATA_FILES:\n                if self._stop_requested:\n                    self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Update cancelled')\n                    return\n\n                self.progress_signal.emit(data_file)\n                url = f\"{GITHUB_RAW_BASE}/{data_file}\"\n                destination = os.path.join(local_data_dir, data_file)\n\n                if self._download_file(url, destination):\n                    downloaded_count += 1\n                else:\n                    error_count += 1\n\n            # Step 2: Get scripts list from GitHub API\n            if self._stop_requested:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Update cancelled')\n                return\n\n            self.progress_signal.emit('scripts list')\n            scripts = self._get_scripts_list()\n\n            if not scripts:\n                # If API fails, try to get scripts from data files\n                logger.warning(\"Could not get scripts list from API, using data files\")\n            else:\n                # Step 3: Download each script\n                for script in scripts:\n                    if self._stop_requested:\n                        self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Update cancelled')\n                        return\n\n                    script_name = script['name']\n                    self.progress_signal.emit(script_name)\n                    destination = os.path.join(local_scripts_dir, script_name)\n\n                    if self._download_file(script['download_url'], destination):\n                        downloaded_count += 1\n                    else:\n                        error_count += 1\n\n            # Report results\n            if error_count > 0:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(\n                    False,\n                    f'Completed with {error_count} errors. Downloaded {downloaded_count} files.'\n                )\n            else:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(\n                    True,\n                    f'Successfully downloaded {downloaded_count} files.'\n                )\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Update error: {e}\")\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, str(e))\n\n\nclass MainWindow(QMainWindow):\n    \"\"\"Main application window.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, lang: str = DEFAULT_LANG):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.lang = lang\n        self.tr = TRANSLATIONS.get(lang, TRANSLATIONS[DEFAULT_LANG])\n        self.scripts = load_scripts(lang)\n        self.worker = None\n        self.update_worker = None\n        self._scripts_load_error = len(self.scripts) == 0\n\n        logger.debug(f\"MainWindow initialized with {len(self.scripts)} scripts\")\n\n        self.init_ui()\n\n    def init_ui(self):\n        \"\"\"Initialize the user interface.\"\"\"\n        self.setWindowTitle(self.tr['window_title'])\n        self.setMinimumSize(800, 600)\n\n        # Check each octet is 0-255\n        octets = ip.split('.')\n        return all(0 <= int(octet) <= 255 for octet in octets)\n\n    def on_script_selection_changed(self, index: int):\n        \"\"\"Handle script selection change in dropdown.\"\"\"\n        if index < 0 or index >= len(self.scripts):\n            self.description_label.setPlainText(\"\")\n            return\n\n        script = self.software_combo.itemData(index)\n        if script:\n            description = script.get('description', '')\n            info = script.get('info', '')\n            # Format: description on first line, info on second line (if present)\n            if info:\n                self.description_label.setPlainText(f\"{description}\\n\\n{info}\")\n            else:\n                self.description_label.setPlainText(description)\n\n    def on_install_clicked(self):\n        \"\"\"Handle install button click.\"\"\"\n        # Get selected script from combo box\n        current_index = self.software_combo.currentIndex()\n        if current_index < 0:\n            QMessageBox.warning(self, \"Error\", self.tr['error_no_script'])\n            return\n\n        script = self.software_combo.itemData(current_index)\n        if not script:\n            QMessageBox.warning(self, \"Error\", self.tr['error_no_script'])\n            return\n\n        script_name = script.get('script_name', '')\n        additional = self.additional_input.text().strip()\n\n        # Clear previous report\n        self.report_text.clear()\n\n        # Disable install button, enable stop button\n        self.install_button.setEnabled(False)\n        self.stop_button.setEnabled(True)\n\n        # load_scripts(lang: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n    \"\"\"Load scripts list from the data file.\"\"\"\n    logger.debug(f\"Loading scripts for language: {lang}\")\n\n    data_file = logger.warning(f\"Data file does not exist: {data_file}\")\n        return []\n\n    try:\n        logger.debug(f\"Opening data file: {data_file}\")\n        with open(data_file, 'r', status_changed = pyqtSignal(str)\n    finished_signal = pyqtSignal(bool, str)\n\n    def __init__(self, server_ip: str, password: str, script_name: str,\n                 additional: str = '', port: int = SSH_DEFAULT_PORT):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.server_ip = server_ip\n        self.password = password\n        self.script_name = script_name\n        self.additional = additional\n        self.port = port\n        self._stop_requested = False\n        self._ssh_client = None\n\n    def request_stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Request the worker to stop.\"\"\"\n        self._stop_requested = True\n        if self._ssh_client:\n            try:\n                self._ssh_client.close()\n            except Exception:\n                pass\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"Execute the installation script via SSH.\"\"\"\n        if not SSH_AVAILABLE:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'SSH library (paramiko) is not installed')\n            return\n\n        try:\n            # Create SSH client\n            self._ssh_client = paramiko.SSHClient()\n            self._ssh_client.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())\n\n            self.status_changed.emit(f\"Connecting to {self.server_ip}:{self.port}...\")\n            self.output_received.emit(f\"Connecting to {self.server_ip}:{self.port} via SSH...\\n\")\n\n            # Connect to the server\n            self._ssh_client.connect(\n                hostname=self.server_ip,\n                port=self.port,\n                username='root',\n                password=self.password,\n                timeout=SSH_DEFAULT_TIMEOUT,\n                look_for_keys=False,\n                allow_agent=False\n            )\n\n            if self._stop_requested:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Stopped by user')\n                return\n\n            # Build the command\n            script_url = f\"{SCRIPTS_BASE_URL}/{self.script_name}.sh\"\n\n            if self.additional:\n                escaped_additional = self.additional.replace(\"'\", \"'\\\"'\\\"'\")\n                command = f\"curl -fsSL -o- {script_url} | bash -s -- '{escaped_additional}'\"\n            else:\n                command = f\"curl -fsSL -o- {script_url} | bash\"\n\n            self.output_received.emit(f\"Executing script: {self.script_name}\\n\")\n            self.output_received.emit(\"-\" * 50 + \"\\n\")\n\n            # Execute the command\n            stdin, stdout, stderr = self._ssh_client.exec_command(command, get_pty=True)\n\n            # Stream output\n            while True:\n                if self._stop_requested:\n                    self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Stopped by user')\n                    return\n\n                line = stdout.readline()\n                if not line:\n                    break\n\n                decoded_line = line if isinstance(line, str) else line.decode('utf-8', errors='replace')\n                clean_line = strip_ansi_codes(decoded_line)\n                self.output_received.emit(clean_line)\n\n            # Read any remaining stderr\n            error_output = stderr.read().decode('utf-8', errors='replace')\n            if error_output:\n                clean_error = strip_ansi_codes(error_output)\n                self.output_received.emit(f\"\\n{clean_error}\")\n\n            # Get exit status\n            exit_status = stdout.channel.recv_exit_status()\n\n            if exit_status != 0:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(False, f'Script exited with status {exit_status}')\n            else:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(True, 'Installation completed successfully')\n\n        except paramiko.AuthenticationException:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'SSH authentication failed. Please check the password.')\n        except paramiko.SSHException as e:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, f'SSH connection error: {str(e)}')\n        except TimeoutError:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, f'Connection to {self.server_ip} timed out')\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, f'Unexpected error: {str(e)}')\n        finally:\n            if self._ssh_client:\n                try:\n                    self._ssh_client.close()\n                except Exception:\n                    pass\n\n\nclass UpdateWorker(QThread):\n    \"\"\"Worker thread for downloading updates from GitHub.\"\"\"\n\n    progress_signal = pyqtSignal(str)  # For status updates\n    finished_signal = pyqtSignal(bool, str)  # success, message\n\n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__()\n        self._stop_requested = False\n\n    def request_stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Request the worker to stop.\"\"\"\n        self._stop_requested = True\n\n    def _download_file(self, url: str, destination: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Download a file from URL to destination.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            logger.debug(f\"Downloading {url} to {destination}\")\n            request = urllib.request.Request(\n                url,\n                headers={'User-Agent': 'Install-Scripts-GUI/1.0'}\n            )\n            with urllib.request.urlopen(request, timeout=30) as response:\n                content = response.read()\n\n            # Ensure directory exists\n            os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(destination), exist_ok=True)\n\n            with open(destination, 'wb') as f:\n                f.write(content)\n\n            logger.debug(f\"Successfully downloaded {url}\")\n            return True\n\n        except urllib.error.URLError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"URL error downloading {url}: {e}\")\n            return False\n        except urllib.error.HTTPError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"HTTP error downloading {url}: {e.code} {e.reason}\")\n            return False\n        except IOError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"IO error saving {destination}: {e}\")\n            return False\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Unexpected error downloading {url}: {e}\")\n            return False\n\n    def _get_scripts_list(self) -> List[Dict[str, str]]:\n        \"\"\"Get list of scripts from GitHub API.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            request = urllib.request.Request(\n                GITHUB_API_SCRIPTS,\n                headers={\n                    'User-Agent': 'Install-Scripts-GUI/1.0',\n                    'Accept': 'application/vnd.github.v3+json'\n                }\n            )\n            with urllib.request.urlopen(request, timeout=30) as response:\n                data = json.loads(response.read().decode('utf-8'))\n\n            # Filter for .sh files\n            scripts = []\n            for item in data:\n                if item.get('type') == 'file' and item.get('name', '').endswith('.sh'):\n                    scripts.append({\n                        'name': item['name'],\n                        'download_url': item['download_url']\n                    })\n\n            logger.debug(f\"Found {len(scripts)} scripts on GitHub\")\n            return scripts\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error fetching scripts list: {e}\")\n            return []\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"Download data files and scripts from GitHub.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            local_data_dir = get_local_data_dir()\n            local_scripts_dir = get_local_scripts_dir()\n            downloaded_count = 0\n            error_count = 0\n\n            # Step 1: Download data files\n            for data_file in DATA_FILES:\n                if self._stop_requested:\n                    self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Update cancelled')\n                    return\n\n                self.progress_signal.emit(data_file)\n                url = f\"{GITHUB_RAW_BASE}/{data_file}\"\n                destination = os.path.join(local_data_dir, data_file)\n\n                if self._download_file(url, destination):\n                    downloaded_count += 1\n                else:\n                    error_count += 1\n\n            # Step 2: Get scripts list from GitHub API\n            if self._stop_requested:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Update cancelled')\n                return\n\n            self.progress_signal.emit('scripts list')\n            scripts = self._get_scripts_list()\n\n            if not scripts:\n                # If API fails, try to get scripts from data files\n                logger.warning(\"Could not get scripts list from API, using data files\")\n            else:\n                # Step 3: Download each script\n                for script in scripts:\n                    if self._stop_requested:\n                        self.finished_signal.emit(False, 'Update cancelled')\n                        return\n\n                    script_name = script['name']\n                    self.progress_signal.emit(script_name)\n                    destination = os.path.join(local_scripts_dir, script_name)\n\n                    if self._download_file(script['download_url'], destination):\n                        downloaded_count += 1\n                    else:\n                        error_count += 1\n\n            # Report results\n            if error_count > 0:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(\n                    False,\n                    f'Completed with {error_count} errors. Downloaded {downloaded_count} files.'\n                )\n            else:\n                self.finished_signal.emit(\n                    True,\n                    f'Successfully downloaded {downloaded_count} files.'\n                )\n\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Update error: {e}\")\n            self.finished_signal.emit(False, str(e))\n\n\nclass MainWindow(QMainWindow):\n    \"\"\"Main application window.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, lang: str = DEFAULT_LANG):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.lang = lang\n        self.tr = TRANSLATIONS.get(lang, TRANSLATIONS[DEFAULT_LANG])\n        self.scripts = load_scripts(lang)\n        self.worker = None\n        self.update_worker = None\n        self._scripts_load_error = len(self.scripts) == 0\n\n        logger.debug(f\"MainWindow initialized with {len(self.scripts)} scripts\")\n\n        self.init_ui()\n\n    def init_ui(self):\n        \"\"\"Initialize the user interface.\"\"\"\n        self.setWindowTitle(self.tr['window_title'])\n        self.setMinimumSize(800, 600)\n\n        # Check each octet is 0-255\n        octets = ip.split('.')\n        return all(0 <= int(octet) <= 255 for octet in octets)\n\n    def on_script_selection_changed(self, index: int):\n        \"\"\"Handle script selection change in dropdown.\"\"\"\n        if index < 0 or index >= len(self.scripts):\n            self.description_label.setPlainText(\"\")\n            return\n\n        script = self.software_combo.itemData(index)\n        if script:\n            description = script.get('description', '')\n            info = script.get('info', '')\n            # Format: description on first line, info on second line (if present)\n            if info:\n                self.description_label.setPlainText(f\"{description}\\n\\n{info}\")\n            else:\n                self.description_label.setPlainText(description)\n\n    def on_install_clicked(self):\n        \"\"\"Handle install button click.\"\"\"\n        # Validate inputs\n        server_ip = self.ip_input.text().strip()\n        if not server_ip:\n            QMessageBox.warning(self, \"Error\", self.tr['error_no_ip'])\n            return\n\n        if not self.validate_ip(server_ip):\n            QMessageBox.warning(self, \"Error\", self.tr['error_invalid_ip'])\n            return\n\n        password = self.password_input.text()\n        if not password:\n            QMessageBox.warning(self, \"Error\", self.tr['error_no_password'])\n            return\n\n        # Get selected script from combo box\n        current_index = self.software_combo.currentIndex()\n        if current_index < 0:\n            QMessageBox.warning(self, \"Error\", self.tr['error_no_script'])\n            return\n\n        script = self.software_combo.itemData(current_index)\n        if not script:\n            QMessageBox.warning(self, \"Error\", self.tr['error_no_script'])\n            return\n\n        script_name = script.get('script_name', '')\n        additional = self.additional_input.text().strip()\n\n        # Clear previous report\n        self.report_text.clear()\n\n        # Disable install button, enable stop button\n        self.install_button.setEnabled(False)\n        self.stop_button.setEnabled(True)\n\n        # Create and start worker thread\n        self.worker = SSHWorker(server_ip, password, script_name, additional)\n        self.worker.output_received.connect(self.on_output_received)\n        self.worker.status_changed.connect(self.on_status_changed)\n        self.worker.finished_signal.connect(self.on_installation_finished)\n        self.worker.start()\n\n    def on_stop_clicked(self):\n        \"\"\"Handle stop button click.\"\"\"\n        if self.worker:\n            self.worker.request_stop()\n            self.stop_button.setEnabled(False)\n\n    def on_output_received(self, text: str):\n        \"\"\"Handle output received from SSH.\"\"\"\n        self.report_text.moveCursor(QTextCursor.MoveOperation.End)\n        self.report_text.insertPlainText(text)\n        # Auto-scroll to bottom\n        scrollbar = self.report_text.verticalScrollBar()\n        scrollbar.setValue(scrollbar.maximum())\n\n    def on_status_changed(self, status: str):\n        \"\"\"Handle status change.\"\"\"\n        self.setWindowTitle(f\"{self.tr['window_title']} - {status}\")\n\n    def on_installation_finished(self, success: bool, message: str):\n        \"\"\"Handle installation completion.\"\"\"\n        self.install_button.setEnabled(True)\n        self.stop_button.setEnabled(False)\n\n        self.report_text.append(\"\\n\" + \"-\" * 50)\n        if success:\n            self.report_text.append(f\"\\n{self.tr['status_completed']}\")\n        else:\n            self.report_text.append(f\"\\n{self.tr['status_error'].format(error=message)}\")\n\n        self.setWindowTitle(self.tr['window_title'])\n        self.worker = None\n\n    def clear_report(self):\n        \"\"\"Clear the report text.\"\"\"\n        self.report_text.clear()\n\n    def on_update_clicked(self):\n        \"\"\"Handle update button click.\"\"\"\n        # Ask for confirmation\n        reply = QMessageBox.question(\n            self,\n            self.tr['update_confirm_title'],\n            self.tr['update_confirm_message'],\n            QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes | QMessageBox.StandardButton.No,\n            QMessageBox.StandardButton.No\n        )\n\n        if reply != QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes:\n            return\n\n        # Disable update button during update\n        self.update_button.setEnabled(False)\n        self.report_text.clear()\n        self.report_text.append(self.tr['update_status_checking'] + \"\\n\")\n\n        # Create and start update worker\n        self.update_worker = UpdateWorker()\n        self.update_worker.progress_signal.connect(self.on_update_progress)\n        self.update_worker.finished_signal.connect(self.on_update_finished)\n        self.update_worker.start()\n\n    def on_update_progress(self, item: str):\n        \"\"\"Handle update progress signal.\"\"\"\n        self.report_text.append(\n            self.tr['update_status_downloading'].format(item=item) + \"\\n\"\n        )\n        # Auto-scroll to bottom\n        scrollbar = self.report_text.verticalScrollBar()\n        scrollbar.setValue(scrollbar.maximum())\n\n    def on_update_finished(self, success: bool, message: str):\n        \"\"\"Handle update completion.\"\"\"\n        self.update_button.setEnabled(True)\n\n        self.report_text.append(\"\\n\" + \"-\" * 50)\n        if success:\n            self.report_text.append(f\"\\n{self.tr['update_status_completed']}\")\n            self.report_text.append(f\"\\n{message}\")\n\n            # Reload scripts with updated data\n            self.scripts = load_scripts(self.lang)\n            self._scripts_load_error = len(self.scripts) == 0\n\n            # Update software combo box\n            current_selection = self.software_combo.currentIndex()\n            self.software_combo.clear()\n            for script in self.scripts:\n                display_text = script.get('name', '')\n                self.software_combo.addItem(display_text, script)\n\n            # Restore selection if possible\n            if 0 <= current_selection < len(self.scripts):\n                self.software_combo.setCurrentIndex(current_selection)\n            elif self.scripts:\n                self.software_combo.setCurrentIndex(0)\n\n            self.on_script_selection_changed(self.software_combo.currentIndex())\n        else:\n            self.report_text.append(\n                f\"\\n{self.tr['update_status_error'].format(error=message)}\"\n            )\n\n        self.update_worker = None\n\n    def on_language_changed(self, index: int):\n        \"\"\"Handle language selection change.\"\"\"\n        new_lang = self.lang_combo.itemData(index)\n        if new_lang == self.lang:\n            return\n\n        # Update language\n        self.lang = new_lang\n        self.tr = TRANSLATIONS.get(new_lang, TRANSLATIONS[DEFAULT_LANG])\n\n        # Reload scripts for the new language\n        self.scripts = load_scripts(new_lang)\n\n        # Update all UI text elements\n        self.update_ui_text()\n\n    def update_ui_text(self):\n        \"\"\"Update all UI text elements with current language.\"\"\"\n        # Window title\n        self.setWindowTitle(self.tr['window_title'])\n\n        # Language label\n        self.lang_label.setText(self.tr['language_label'])\n\n        # Input labels\n        self.ip_label.setText(self.tr['server_ip'])\n        self.password_label.setText(self.tr['server_password'])\n        self.additional_label.setText(self.tr['additional_info'])\n\n        # Software label\n        self.software_label.setText(self.tr['software_list'])\n\n        # Update software combo box with scripts in new language\n        current_selection = self.software_combo.currentIndex()\n        self.software_combo.clear()\n        for script in self.scripts:\n            display_text = script.get('name', '')\n            self.software_combo.addItem(display_text, script)\n\n        # Restore selection if possible\n        if 0 <= current_selection < len(self.scripts):\n            self.software_combo.setCurrentIndex(current_selection)\n        elif self.scripts:\n            self.software_combo.setCurrentIndex(0)\n\n        # Update description\n        self.on_script_selection_changed(self.software_combo.currentIndex())\n\n        # Update buttons\n        self.update_button.setText(self.tr['update_button'])\n        self.install_button.setText(self.tr['install_button'])\n        self.stop_button.setText(self.tr['stop_button'])\n        self.clear_button.setText(self.tr['clear_button'])\n\n        # Update report label\n        self.report_label.setText(self.tr['report_title'])\n\n    def closeEvent(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Handle window close event.\"\"\"\n        if self.worker and self.worker.isRunning():\n            reply = QMessageBox.question(\n                self, 'Confirm Exit',\n                'Installation is in progress. Are you sure you want to exit?',\n                QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes | QMessageBox.StandardButton.No,\n                QMessageBox.StandardButton.No\n            )\n\n            if reply == QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes:\n                self.worker.request_stop()\n                self.worker.wait(2000)\n                event.accept()\n            else:\n                event.ignore()\n        else:\n            event.accept()\n\n\ndef setup_logging(debug: bool = False) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Configure logging for the application.\"\"\"\n    # Configure root logger\n    logging.basicConfig(level=level, format=log_format)\n\n    # Also log to file if in debug mode\n    if debug:\n        try:\n            # Get a writable directory for the log file\n            if getattr(sys, 'frozen', False):\n                # For frozen executables, use user's home directory\n                log_dir = os.path.expanduser('~')\n            else:\n                # For development, use current directory\n                log_dir = os.getcwd()\n\n            log_file = os.path.join(log_dir, 'install_scripts_debug.log')\n            file_handler = logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8')\n            file_handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)\n            file_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter(log_format))\n            logging.getLogger().addHandler(file_handler)\n            logger.info(f\"Debug logging enabled, log file: {log_file}\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.warning(f\"Could not create log file: {e}\")\n\n\ndef parse_args():\n    \"\"\"Parse command-line arguments.\"\"\"\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description='Install Scripts GUI - PyQt6 Application for installing software on remote servers'\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        '--lang',\n        type=str,\n        default=DEFAULT_LANG,\n        choices=['ru', 'en'],\n        help='Language for the interface (default: ru)'\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        '--debug',\n        action='store_true',\n        help='Enable debug logging (also via INSTALL_SCRIPTS_DEBUG=1 env var)'\n    )\n    return parser.parse_args()\n\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main entry point.\"\"\"\n    args = parse_args()\n\n    # `urllib.request` and `urllib.error` for HTTP downloads\n\n2. **Added configuration constants**:\n   - `GITHUB_RAW_BASE` - Base URL for raw file downloads\n   - `GITHUB_API_SCRIPTS` - GitHub API endpoint for listing scripts\n   - `DATA_FILES` - List of data files to download\n   - `LOCAL_DATA_DIR_NAME` - Name of local data directory\n\n3. **Added translations** for both Russian and English:\n   - `update_button`: \"Обновить\" / \"Update\"\n   - `update_status_checking`: Status messages for checking\n   - `update_status_downloading`: Download progress messages\n   - `update_status_completed`: Completion messages\n   - `update_status_error`: Error messages\n   - `update_confirm_title` / `update_confirm_message`: Confirmation dialog\n\n4. **Added helper functions**:\n   - `get_local_data_dir()`: Returns platform-appropriate local data directory (`~/.local/share/install_scripts_data/` on Linux, `%LOCALAPPDATA%/install_scripts_data/` on Windows)\n   - `get_local_scripts_dir()`: Returns local scripts subdirectory\n\n5. **Modified `get_data_file_path()`**: Now checks local data directory first (for updates), then falls back to bundled files\n\n6. **Added `UpdateWorker` class**: A `QThread` subclass that:\n   - Downloads data files from GitHub\n   - Fetches scripts list via GitHub API\n   - Downloads all scripts\n   - Emits progress and completion signals\n\n7. **Added UI elements**:\n   - \"Update\" button next to language selector\n   - Confirmation dialog before updating\n\n8. **Added handler methods**:\n   - `on_update_clicked()`: Shows confirmation and starts update\n   - `on_update_progress()`: Updates report text with download progress\n   - `on_update_finished()`: Handles completion and reloads scripts\n\n9. **Updated `update_ui_text()`**: Added update button text update\n\n10. **Updated `closeEvent()`**: Added check for running update worker\n\n### Test file created:\n- `experiments/test_update_functionality.py`: Tests the download functionality without Qt dependencies\n\n### How it works:\n1. User clicks \"Update\" button\n2. Confirmation dialog appears\n3. Data files (`data_ru.json`, `data_en.json`) are downloaded to local data directory\n4. Scripts list is fetched via GitHub API\n5. All scripts are downloaded to local scripts directory\n6. Scripts list is reloaded from the updated data files\n\n### Important design decision:\nThe implementation uses a **separate local data directory** (`~/.local/share/install_scripts_data/`) instead of modifying the bundled files. This is essential for the `onefile` mode because:\n- In `onefile` mode, PyInstaller extracts files to a read-only temporary directory\n- The local data directory is always writable and persists between application runs\n- `get_data_file_path()` checks the local directory first, giving priority to updates\n\nThe commit is ready locally (`e4de2f0`) but cannot be pushed due to expired GitHub authentication token. The implementation has been tested and all non-GUI tests pass."
